       <div class="section" id="introduction"> 
        <span id="intro"></span>
        <h1><a class="toc-backref" href="#id4">Introduction</a></h1> 
        <p>This PEP contains the index of all Python Enhancement Proposals, known as PEPs. PEP numbers are assigned by the PEP editors, and once assigned are never changed [<a class="reference internal" href="#id2">1</a>]. The version control history [<a class="reference internal" href="#id3">2</a>] of the PEP texts represent their historical record.</p> 
       </div> 
       <div class="section" id="index-by-category"> 
        <span id="by-category"></span>
        <h1><a class="toc-backref" href="#id5">Index by Category</a></h1> 
        <div class="section" id="meta-peps-peps-about-peps-or-processes"> 
         <span id="by-category-meta"></span>
         <h2><a class="toc-backref" href="#id6">Meta-PEPs (PEPs about PEPs or Processes)</a></h2> 
         <table border="1" class="docutils"> 
          <colgroup> 
           <col width="2%"> 
           <col class="num" width="4%"> 
           <col width="54%"> 
           <col width="40%"> 
          </colgroup> 
          <thead valign="bottom"> 
           <tr>
            <th class="head">

       <div class="section" id="pep-types-key"> 
        <span id="type-key"></span>
        <h1><a class="toc-backref" href="#id17">PEP Types Key</a></h1> 
        <blockquote> 
         <p>I - Informational PEP</p> 
         <p>P - Process PEP</p> 
         <p>S - Standards Track PEP</p> 
        </blockquote> 
       </div> 
       <div class="section" id="pep-status-key"> 
        <span id="status-key"></span>
        <h1><a class="toc-backref" href="#id18">PEP Status Key</a></h1> 
        <blockquote> 
         <p>A - Accepted (Standards Track only) or Active proposal</p> 
         <p>D - Deferred proposal</p> 
         <p>F - Final proposal</p> 
         <p>P - Provisional proposal</p> 
         <p>R - Rejected proposal</p> 
         <p>S - Superseded proposal</p> 
         <p>W - Withdrawn proposal</p> 
        </blockquote> 
       </div>
